 yoga hamen baithne kaa tarika, pranayam tathaa dhyaan sanyukt rup se sikhaata he
 Regular practitioners receive innumerable benefits
 swasth main laabh, maansik shakti, shaareerik shakti, sharir kii tut foot se raksha or sharir kaa shuddh hona jaise kai laabh hamen yoga se milte hai
 Let's know about 21 yogasanas and also how to do them
 1-ardh chandrasana-is asana ko karte samay sharir kii sthiti ardh chandra jaisi ho jaati he isliye ise ardhachandrasana kehete he
 Ardha means half and Chandrasana means posture similar to Chandra
 is asana ko khadey hokar kiya jaataa he
 Ardha Chandrasana is also called Half Moon Pose in English
 yah asana saamaanya streacing or balencing pos he jo khaskar qamar ke nichle hisse, pet or seene ke liye laabhadaayak he
 By doing this asana, stress is relieved
 ardhachandrasana kaa sahi tarika-ise karne ke liye sabase pehle donon pairon kii edi-panjon ko milakar khadey ho jaaen
 Both hands should be adjacent to the waist and keep your neck straight
 phir dhire dhire donon pairon ko ek duusare se kareeb ek se dedh fit kii duuri par rakhen
 Keep in mind that while practicing this asana, your spine is straight
 iske uparaant daaen haath ko upar uthaaen or kandhe ke samanaantar laaen
 Your palm should be facing towards the sky
 ise karte samay dhyaan rahe ki aapkaa baayan haath aapaki qamar par hi rahe
 Now bend to the left, during this time your left hand will slide down on its own
 yaad rahe ki baayen haath kii hatheli ko baayen pair se alag na hatane paae
 Remain in this position for 30-40 seconds, then slowly return to normal
 agar ise pehali baar kar rahe he to jitna ho sake utana hi jhuken
 Do the same procedure on the other side
 2-bhujang asana-sabase pehle apane pet ke bal se let jaaen
 Now bring your palms in line with your shoulder
 is dauraan apane donon paanvon ke bich kii duuri ko kam karen saath hi paanv ko sidhaa tathaa tana hua rakhen
 Now, while breathing, raise the front part of the body to the navel
 is dauraan dhyaan rakhen ki apni qamar ke upar zyada stretch na aa paae
 Keep this state of yours according to your ability
 yoga kaa abhyaas karte samay dhime dhime saans bharen or phir choden
 Return to the starting posture, exhaling a deep breath
 is tarah is asana kaa ek puraa chakra khatm hua
 Repeat this as per your ability
 3-bal asana-bal kaa arth he- shishu yaa baccha, balasana main ham ek shishu kii tarah vajra asana lekar haathon or sharir ko aage kii ore jhukaate he
 This asana is very easy, but also very beneficial
 qamar kii mansapeshiyon ko aaraam detaa he or ye asana kabz ko bhi dur karata he
 This asana which calms the mind, calms the nervous system
 balasana (shishuasana) karne kii prakriya-apni ediyon par baith jaaen, edi par kulhon ko rakhen, aage kii ore jhuke or maathe ko jameen par lagaaein
 Keep the hands on both sides of the body on the ground, extending the palm towards the sky (if it is not comfortable then you keep the forehead relaxed by placing the other palm on top of one palm
 )
 Gently press the thighs from the chest
 sthiti ko banaaye rakhen
 Get up slowly and sit on the heel and straighten the spine slowly
 vishram karen
 4-margar Asana - Come on your knees and hands and make the body a table in many ways
 apni peeth se mej kaa upree hissaa banaaen or haath or pair se mej ke chaaron pair banaaen
 With your hands just below the shoulders, keep the palms sticking to the ground and keep the gap between the knees as the tendons
 gardan sidhi nazren saamne rakhen
 Breathing, move your chin upward to the head, press your navel towards the ground and move the lower part of your waist towards the ceiling
 donon putathon ko sikod len
 Keep this position and take long deep breaths and keep going
 ab isaki vipareet sthiti karenge
 While exhaling, apply the chin to the chest and raise the back as high as possible in the bow shape, leaving the tendons loose
 is sthiti ko kuch samay tak banaaen rakhen or phir pehle ki tarah mejanuma sthiti main aa jaaen
 Repeat this process five to 6 times and relax
 5-nataraj asana-bhagwaan shiv ke naam par is asana kaa naam rakhaa gaya he
 Initially, it may be difficult to do it, but it can be done easily by its regular practice
 sabase pehle aaraam kii mudra main khadey ho jaaen
 Install the weight of the body on the left leg and bend the right knee slowly and lift the leg above the ground
 daaen pair ko modakar apane peeche le jaaen
 Hold the right ankle with the right hand
 baayen baanh ko kandhe kii oonchaai main uthaaen
 While exhaling, press the left foot on the ground and bend forward
 daaen pair ko sharir se dur le jaaen
 Keep the head and neck aligned with the spinal cord
 is mudra main 15 se 30 second tak bane rahen
 This will improve your body balance and make your body more and more flexible
 is asana se haath- pairon main rakt sanchaar behatar hoga, nervas system behatar hota he
 6-gomukh posture - Gomukh posture is the yoga to make the body shapely and strong
 yoga kii is mudra ko baithkar kiya jaataa he
 This posture basically involves exercise of both hands, waist and spinal cord
 gomukh asana striyon ke liye bahut hi laabhprad vyaayaam he
 Sit with a plate
 apane baayen pair ko mode kar baayen talave ko daaen hips ke peeche laaen
 Bring the right sole behind the left hips by bending the right leg
 apane hatheliyon ko pairon par rakhen
 Press the hips lightly downwards and keep the upper part of the body straight and make the head straight and full
 baayin kohni ko mode kar haathon ko peeche kii ore le jaaen
 Breathing out, raise the right hand up
 daayi kohni ko mode kar daaen haath ko peeche kii ore le jaaen
 Add fingers of both hands together
 donon haathon ko halke se apni disha main khinchen
 7-halasana-halasana In Halasana, the body is kept in a plow posture
 is asana ke liye sharir kaa lacheela hona bahut aavashyak hota he
 Lie flat on your back on the floor and keep both your hands straight on the ground in a completely relaxed posture
 lambii saans lete hue pet kii mansapeshiyon ke sahare apane pairon ko farsh se upar uthaaen or donon pairon ko 90 ansh ke kone par khadey rakhen
 Breathing normally, raise your hips and back from the floor with the help of hands
 ab apane pairon ko sir ke upar se le jate hue 180 degree ke kone par mode jab tak ki aapke pairon kii ungliyaan farsh se nahin chhu jaati hai
 Your back should be perpendicular to the floor
 is mudra main hone main shuru main aapako mushkil jarur hogi lekin thode praytn ke baad aap ise aasaani se kar sakate hai
 Do this process slowly and comfortably
 lekin saath main yah bhi dhyaan rakhen ki aapako apane gardan par dabaav nahin daalana he naa hi isse jameen kii ore dhakka dena he
 Now come to normal state and give the body some rest
 saans lete rahen or relax mahasoos karen
 8-bridge dam Asan-bridge dam Yoga posture makes the spinal cord flexible as well as removes tension from the neck
 peeth ke bal let jaaen
 Keep the soles firmly on the ground by bending the knees
 sharir ke donon taraf baahon ko bhoomi se lagaakar rakhen
 In this state, the palms should rest on the ground
 saans chhodte hue ridh kii haddiyon ko khinche or qamar ko zamin kii ore dhire se dabaaen
 Taking a deep breath, press the feet towards the ground and raise the pedu as high as possible
 is mudra main 30 second se 1 minute tak bane rahen
 Breathing out, slowly return to normal
 9- rocking chair yoga-rocking chair yoga karne se ridh kii haddiyon main urja kaa sanchaar hota he
 Also, blood circulation in the body is fast
 10-sukhasana-sukhasana main donon pairon ko ek cross kii mudra main dabaakar rakhaa jaataa he jise camel mudra bhi kehete hai
 It is a suitable posture for meditation
 samtal jameen par aasaan bichhaakar palathi modakar baith jaaen
 Keep your head neck and back straight, not bending them
 kandhon ko thodaa dhilaa choden
 Keep both hands on knees and palms up
 sir ko thodaa upar uthaaen or ankhen band kar len
 Now concentrate on your breathing and keep taking long and deep breaths
 is asana ko kabhi bhi ekant main baithkar 5-10 minute tak kar sakate hai
 If you are doing this yoga spiritually, then do it in the east or north direction
 11
 Namaskar Asana - Namaskar Asana is performed at the beginning of any asana
 ye kaaphi saral he
 12-tadasana-first of all stand upright
 phir apane donon pair ko aapas main milakar rakhen or donon haathon ko sidhaa qamar se sataakar rakhen
 Your body should remain stable at this time
 yani ki aapke donon pairo par sharir kaa vajan saamaan hona chahie
 Now slowly bring the hands parallel to the shoulders
 ab donon hatheliyon kii anguliyon ko milakar sir ke upar le jaaen
 Now, while breathing, pull your hands upwards, until you feel a stretch in your shoulders and chest
 isi vakt pairon kii edi ko bhi upar uthaaen or saavdhaanee se panjon ke bal khadey ho jaaen
 Now put finger locks and fold the hands claws upwards
 is vakt aapaki gardan sidhi honi chahie or hatheliyaan aasmaan kii ore hona chahie
 Keep in mind that the balance of the body is maintained on your toes
 kuch der is sthiti main rukne ke baad saans chhodte hue haathon ko waapas sir ke upar le aaen
 Slowly, keep the ankles on the ground too and bring both hands down and come back to the resting position of the previous position, which is close to the waist
 is asana ko niyamit kam se kam 10 baar karen
 13-triangle mudra-triangle Asana is practiced standing up
 yah asana parshv konasana se miltaa julata he
 This yoga exercises the hips, legs, ankles, legs and chest
 yah mudra qamar ke liye bhi laabhprad he
 How should one practice this mudra
 is mudra kii avasthaa kya he evam isse kya laabh miltaa he aaiye ise dekhen
 Stand in a relaxed posture
 daaen pair ko 3 se 5 feet failaaen
 Turn left leg 45 degrees and right leg 90 degrees
 saans lete hue kandhon kii oonchaai main baahon ko failaaen
 In this situation, the palms should be placed in the direction of the ground
 hips ko peeche le jaaen or sharir ke upree bhaag ko daayin ore laaen
 Exhaling, move the right palm behind the right leg
 baayen haath ko chat kii disha main upar le jaaen
 Try turning the head in the direction of the left hand
 is avasthaa main merudand sidhaa or gardan relax hona chahie
 Remain in this posture for 10 to 30 seconds
 14-konasana-konasana karne main jitna aasaan he, sharir ke liye utana hi laabhakaarak bhi he
 Keep a gap of 2 feet between the legs
 donon pair par baraabar bhaar santulit karen
 Inhale, move both hands over the head with the spread and join the palms
 angalio ko aapas main jod kar gumbadnuma avasthaa main hatho ko rakhen
 Keep in mind that hands go touching your ears
 shwaas baahar chhodte hue daahine ore jhuken
 Note that the hands do not turn from the elbows
 zamin par pair se dabaav banaae rakhen
 Sway the pelvis and stay
 is sthiti main bane rahen
 Maintain a bending stretch in the body
 is sthiti main rahete hue gahari shwaas len or choden
 Inhale, stand back in normal position
 shwaas chhodte hue donon haath neeche laaen
 Repeat the same process on the left
 15-ushtasana-"ushtr" ek sanskrit bhashaa kaa shabd he or iskaa arth oont hota he
 Ustrasana is called "camel Pose" in English
 ustrasana ek madhyavarti peeche jhukne-yoga asana he jo anahath (hryday chakra) ko kholta he
 This asana brings flexibility in the body, gives strength to the body and increases digestive power
 mat par ghutane ke sahare baith jaaen or kulhe par donon haathon ko rakhen
 The knees should be parallel to the shoulders and the soles of the feet should be towards the sky
 saans lete hue merudand ko puronitamb kii ore khinche jaise ki naabhi se khinchaa ja rahaa he
 Stay neutral sitting without straining your neck
 isi sthiti main kuch saanse lete rahen
 Exhale and return to your initial position
 haathon ko waapas apni qamar par laaen or sidhe ho jaaen
 16-vajrasana - The practice of this asana makes the body strong
 yah ek saadhnaatmak mudra hai
 This is the only posture that can be done even after eating
 is asana ko din yaa shaam donon vakt kar sakate hai
 To perform Vajrasana, place the carpets on a clean flat area
 phir is par ghutanon ke bal baithe tathaa panjon ko peeche failaakar ek pair ke anguuthe ko duusare anguuthe par rakh den
 In this posture, your knees should be close together but the ankles should be different
 aapkaa nitamb donon panjo ke bich main hona chahie or ediyaan kulhon kii taraf
 Now place your palms on the knees
 aap apni kshamta ke anusaar vajrasana kaa abhyaas kiijie
 Come back to normal later
 vajrasana karne ke liye bhojan ke baad pehle 5 minute kaa samay len, phir ise karen
 17-vriksasana-vriksasana means tree-like posture
 is asana ko khadey hokar kiya jaataa he
 Like Nataraja posture, this asana is also very beneficial for physical balance and stand up straight to do Vrikshasana
 sharir kaa bhaar baayen pair par daaliye or daane pair ko modie
 Bring the sole of the right foot above the knees and apply it with the left foot
 donon hatheliyon ko prarthana mudra main chaati ke paas lie
 Press the left foot off the soles of your right foot
 baayen pair ke talave ko zamin kii ore dabaaie
 Take your hands above the head while breathing
 sir ko sidhaa rakhie or saamne kii ore dekhie
 Stay in this posture for 15 to 30 seconds
 donon taraf is mudra ko 2 se 5 baar duharaayiye
 18-to do dandasana-dandasana, first place blankets etc
 in a clean place
 ab sidhaa tan kar baith jaaiye or donon pairon ko chahare ke samaanaantar ek duusare se sataakar sidhaa rakhen
 Keep the head very straight
 apane pairon kii ungaliyon ko andar kii ore moden or talvon ko baahar kii ore dhakka den
 19-downward dog posture - Downward swan posture is symbolic of leaning forward like a dog (schwann / Swan), hence it is called downward swan posture
 apane haathon or pairon ke bal aa jaaen
 Bring the body to the position of a table
 aapaki peeth mez kii upree hisse kii tarah ho or donon haath or pair mez ke pair kii tarah
 Exhale, raising the waist
 apane ghutane or kohni ko majbootee dete hue sidhe karte hue) apane sharir se ulta v aakaar banaaen
 Hands should be as far as the shoulders
 pair qamar ke duuri ke baraabar or ek duusare ke samanaantar hon
 The toes should be exactly in front
 apni hatheliyon ko jameen par dabaaen, kandhon ke sahare ise majbootee pradaan karen
 Keeping the neck taut, touch the ears with the arms
 lambi gahari shwaas len,adhomukh swaan kii avasthaa main bane rahen
 Keep your eyes on the navel
 shwaas chhodte hue ghutane ko mode or waapas mez vaali sthiti main aa jaaen
 veg out
 20-savasana-ise karte samay aapako relax mahasoos karnaa he
 Now lie on your back and keep in mind that in this state your feet should be perfectly straight on the ground
 apane donon haathon ko sharir se kam se kam 5 inch kii duuri par rakhen
 Place the hands in such a way that the palms of both the hands are in the direction of the sky
 ab sharir ke har ang ko aapako dhilaa chhodana he, or aankhon ko bhi band karnaa he
 Take small breaths
 is vakt aapkaa puraa dhyaan shwaanson par hona chahie
 Do not let any other thoughts come to your mind
 is aasaan ko karte vakt yadi aapako qamar yaa ridh main kisi prakaar kii pareshaani mahasoos hoti he to ghutane ke neeche kambal yaa takiya rakh sakate hai
 21-utkat Asana - Keep both feet together and stand upright
 pairon kii ediyaan or ungliyaan bhi milakar rakhen
 Sit down with both knees bent and lift the ankles so that the balance of the entire body remains on both the toes
 donon ghutanon ko milakar rakhie
 Try to keep the spine straight
 donon haathon ko bagal main zamin se sataakar rakhen taaki santulan banane main suvidha ho
 After this, put both elbows on the thighs and put the fingers of hands together under the chin
 saans ke prati sajag rahen or santulan banaae rakhane kaa prayaas karen
 Stop in this position for one to two minutes and concentrate on one point in front
 iske baad phir se khadey ho jaaen

 ' ham sabhi is baat ko acchhee tarah jaanate hai ki hamaare fasebuk feed main vahi saamagree pradarshit hoti he jis tarah kii saamagree ko ham like karte hai, yaa coment or share karte hai
 We call this the resonance effect
 yah bhi sahi he ki fasebuk par dikhne vaale feed main se ham har ek post ko like yaa share nahin karte bhale hi vah hamen pasand ho
 Even if you do not have any activity on Facebook, Facebook will now be aware of whether the content appearing in your feed is interesting to you or not
 'tenk crunch' kii report ke mutabik fasebuk apni pranali main sudhaar kar rahaa he, jisase use yah pataa chal sakegaa ki aap apane feed main maujuud kisi post par kitna samay vyateet kar rahe hai, phir chaahe aap kisi post ko like, share or coment karen yaa na karen
 As soon as you stop for a moment on a post, the Facebook timer starts indirectly
 agar aap kisi post par tasviir dekhne, coment padhane se adhik samay vyateet karte hai to fasebuk ise sanket (aapaki pasandida saamagree) samajhegaa
 With this change, Facebook will know about your interest without your activity

 gorakhpur alaava maharajaganj or shravasti se lekar gonda ke kai gaanvon main vanatangiya samudaay ke log rahete hai

 The British were hopeful that the pegs of cut trees would make the forests ready again, but this did not happen
 iske baad jangal kshetra main paudhon kii dekharekh karne ke liye majdoor rakhe gaye the

" kasuri kaa yah bhi maananaa he ki mujahidin kii gatividhiyon ke prati shuruaati samarthan ke baavjood pashchim or khaastaur par pakistan ko is jihad ke liye baari keemat chukaani pad rahi he or ye ab bhi iske palatwaar kaa shikaar ban rahe hai
 In a recent issue of Equator Line magazine, he wrote, "over time the West and Pakistan had to deal with the growing relationship between terrorist groups with different opinions
 pakistan ko yah bhi pataa chalaa ki kashmir main lard rahe kuch samooh uske apane nagarikon or suraksha balon par bhi aasaani se hamale bol sakate hai
 '' is patrika main unhone likhaa, ‘‘kai maamalon main khufia agency or kanoon pravartan agenciyon ko bhi nishaanaa banaaya gaya
 Public opinion in Pakistan is now turning against the activities of violent groups, irrespective of any reason for this violence
 ’’ patrika ke liye lekh likhane waalon main sabhi pakistani mul ke log hai
 Kasuri said that it is now widely accepted in the middle class people and large sections of the media that Kashmir and other issues with India cannot be resolved through violence of non-governmental elements and although these activities have led to international level But it has caught the attention of the people but after the 9 / 11 attacks, it became clear that the international community is losing patience towards such activities
 kasuri ne likhaa, ‘‘yah ahsaas ho gaya he ki pakistan or bharat ko kashmir or anya muddon ko sulajhane ke liye baatcheet ke jariye samaadhaan nikaalnaa hoga
 i do not want to give the message that at the time when i took office, the feeling of cooperation towards jihadi groups in all sections was over
 lekin kashmir ke mudde ke prati pakistan kii drudh patibaddhta ke kaaran kuch virgon main jihadiyon kii gatividhiyon ke prati sahanubhuti kaa tatv bahut kam lekin ,hameshaa rahegaa
 '' kasuri ke anusaar, pakistan main kattarpanth ke udai ke kai kaaran hai or is mudde ko kam se kam chaar paridrishyon main dekhnaa madadgaar ho saktaa he
 "the first scenario is about the political and constitutional struggle of Pakistan to create a new regime after partition
" isane ulema kii bhoomika ko pakkaa karte hue general jiya-ul-haq ke tahat iskaa vistaar hone diya
 As a result, the extremist forces later strengthened
 ’’tippaniyan "the second scenario was played in opposing it after 1979, after the Iranian revolution, the attack on Afghanistan by the Soviet Union and Pakistan with the help of the entire Muslim community led by the entire Western world, China and Saudi Arabia
" The role is after
 isane charampanthiyon or aatankiyon ko majboot kiya
 '' unhone likhaa, ‘‘pakistan or bharat ke bich ke samikarnon ne pakistan ke bheetar udaar tatwon kii keemat par pratikriyaavaadi tatwon ko majboot karne main madad kii
 The fourth factor is considered to be the situation in Pakistan after the zarb-e-azb operation
 yah aaparishan pakistani sena ne sangh prashasit kabyli ilaakon main sharan liye hue or apni gatividhiyon ke liye puri avasanrachana taiyaar kar chuke aatankiyon ko mitaane ke liye chalaaya tha
 '' bharat-paak sambandhon ke bare main unhone kaha, ‘‘pakistan or bharat ke sambandh kaa pakistan main muslimon ke bich charampanthi tatwon par ek asar padataa he
 Apart from this, the tense state of the Kashmir valley also acts as a temptation and encourages extremist elements to 'jihad to liberate their fellow Muslims'
 ’’ unka maananaa he ki donon deshon ke bich sambandh saamaanya hone se pakistan kii bahultavaadi or udaaravaadi takaton ko madad milegi or iske saath hi donon hi deshon main alpsankhyakon kii sthiti main sudhaar main bhi madad milegi
 Kasuri also believes that despite initial support for the Mujahideen's activities, the West, and especially Pakistan, are paying a heavy price for this jihad and are still falling prey to its counterattack
 equater line patrika ke haalia ank main unhone likhaa, ‘‘samay ke saath pashchim or pakistan ko vibhinn maton vaale aatanki samoohon ke bich bad rahe sambandhon se nipatna padaa
 Pakistan also came to know that some groups fighting in Kashmir can easily attack their own civilians and security forces
 ’’ He wrote in this magazine, "in many cases, intelligence agencies and law enforcement agencies were also targeted
 pakistan main janata kii raay ab hinsak samoohon kii gatividhiyon ke khilaaf hone lagi he phir chaahe yah hinsa kisi bhi kaaran se kyon na kii ja rahi ho
 "people who write articles for the magazine are all people of Pakistani origin
" kasuri ne kaha ki madhyavarg ke logon or media ke bade tabakon main ab yah baat vyapak taur par maani jane lagi he ki bharat ke saath kashmir or anya mudde sarkaar se itar tatwon kii hinsa ke jariye nahin sulajhaaye ja sakate or haalanki in gatividhiyon ne antarrashtriya str par logon kaa dhyaan khinchaa he lekin 9 / 11 ke hamalon ke baad yah spasht ho gaya ki antarrashtriya samudaay aisi gatividhiyon ke prati dhairya kho baitha he
 Kasuri wrote, "it has been realized that Pakistan and India have to find solutions through dialogue to resolve Kashmir and other issues
" main yah sandesh nahin dena chahta ki jis samay maine padbhaar sambhala, us samay sabhi virgon main jihadi samoohon ke prati sahyog kii bhaavana khatm ho gai
 But due to Pakistan's strong commitment to the issue of Kashmir, there will always be little, but little element of sympathy for the activities of jihadis in some sections
 ’’ According to Kasuri, there are many reasons for the rise of fundamentalism in Pakistan and it may be helpful to look at this issue in at least four scenarios
 ‘‘pehla paridrishy vibhaajan ke baad nayaa shashan khadaa karne ke liye pakistan ke raajnneetik or sanvaidhanik sangharsh kaa he
 It confirmed the role of the ulema and allowed it to expand under General zia-ul-haq
 jiske falswaroop baad main charampanthi takatein majboot huin
 '' Comments ‘‘doosraa paridrishy varsh 1979 ke baad yani irani kranti ke baad kii sthiti main soviet sangh dwaara afghanistan par kiye gaye hamale or pakistan dwaara puure pashchimi jagat, china evam saudi arab ke netritv main puure muslim samudaay kii madad se iskaa virodh karne main nibhaai gai bhoomika ke baad kaa he
 This strengthened the extremists and the terrorists
 ’’ He wrote, "the equations between Pakistan and India helped strengthen the reactionary elements at the expense of liberal elements within Pakistan
" chauthaa kaarak jarb-e-ajb oparation ke baad pakistan kii sthiti ko mana jaataa he
 This operation was carried out by the Pakistani army to take refuge in the federally administered tribal areas and to eradicate the terrorists who have prepared the entire infrastructure for their activities

 '' pradhanmantri karyaalay ne kaha he ki pradhanmantri har vakt duty par rahete hai or purv pradhanmantriyon kii chuttee kaa koi record uske paas uplabdh nahin he
 The PMO responded when an RTI application from the Prime Minister's Office and the Cabinet Secretariat sought a copy of the holiday rules and procedures for the country's Prime Minister
 piemo ne artiai jawaab main kaha, ‘‘pradhanmantri ko har vakt duty par maujuud kaha ja saktaa he
 The person requesting was also to know whether former Prime Ministers Manmohan Singh, Atal Bihari Vajpayee, HD Deve Gowda, Indra Kumar Gujral, PV Narasimha Rao, Chandrasekhar, VP Singh and Rajiv Gandhi had taken any leave and whether There is a record artiai jawaab main bataaya gaya ki purv pradhanmantriyon ke avkaash ricard ke bare main soochna is karyaalay dwaara rakhe jane vaale ricard kaa hissaa nahin he
 However, it may be mentioned that the current Prime Minister Narendra Modi has not taken any leave since he took office
 isi tarah kii ek artiai arji aavedak ne cabinet sachivalay jaise anya praadhikaar ko daayar kar yah jaananaa chaha ki kya unke paas purv pradhanmantriyon ke avkaash or sarkaar ke pramukh ke liye is silsile main niyamon kii koi soochna he
 The comments iskaa koi jawaab nahin diya gaya or arji grahamantralay ko bhej di gai jisane ise piemo ko bhej diya
 The PMO said it has no record of the leave of former prime ministers
 (hedline ke alaava, is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he, yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) pradhanmantri karyaalay or cabinet sachivalay se ek artiai arji ke jariye desh ke pradhanmantri ke liye avkaash niyamon evam karypranali kii ek prati maange jane par piemo ne yah jawaab diya
 The PMO said in an RTI reply, "the Prime Minister can be said to be on duty at all times
" ’’ arji dene vaala vyakti yah bhi jaananaa tha ki kya purv pradhanmantri manmohan singh, atal bihari vaajapeyi, ech di devgauda, indra kumaar gujral, pivi narsingh raav, chandrashekhar, veepi singh or rajeev gandhi ne koi chuttee lee thi tathaa kya is bare main koi ricard he
 The RTI reply stated that information about the leave records of former Prime Ministers is not a part of the records kept by this office
 haalanki, yah zikr kiya ja saktaa he ki padbhaar sanbhaalane ke baad se maujuuda pradhanmantri narendra modi ne koi chuttee nahin lee he
 a similar RTI application was filed by another authority like the Cabinet Secretariat to find out if they had any information about the rules in this regard for ex-prime ministers' holidays and heads of government
 tippaniyan No reply was given and the application was sent to the Home Ministry which sent it to the PMO

 ) tii-20 formet main srilanka ke captain lasith malinga ne chot ke chalate captaini chhod di he

 tippaniyan Angelo Mathews will be led by Sri Lanka in place of Malinga
 malinga ne asia cap ke dauraan world tii-20 ke baad cricket se sanyas lene kii khabar kaa khandan bhi nahin kiya tha

 kitaab lekhak kaa cinema ke lekhak kunwar narayan hai

 vaani prakaashan se prakashit is kitaab kii keemat 495 ru
 is
 kavi kunwar narayan ke cinema par lekhon kaa sangrah he kitaab lekhak kaa cinema
 There are 26 articles in the first part of this book divided into two sections and 8 in the second i
e
 34 articles collected in total
 yah kahana atishyokti na hoga ki ye maatr lekh nahin balki vishwa cinema par likhe, 34 kitabon ke saar hai
 These articles are rare articles written from 1976 to 2008 in newspapers and magazines like Chhayanat, Sarika, Dinman, Dharmyug, Femina, Navbharat Times, Jansatta and Swatantra Bharat
 geet chaturvedi ne bade shram se ise sampadit kiya he

 Especially in the early stages, cinema invites not only to look at the fine analysis of the works of great filmmakers, who are critics and writers of other genres, but also to read this visual mode
 in samikshaon main lekhkeey drushtikon pramukh he
 Its rationale is related to the cinema movement in which the New Wave was linked to literature
 is tarah se ye samikshaayen film or sahitya ke antarsambandhon ko bhi karine se anderline karti hai or hamen unhen mahasoos karne kaa nyauta detii hai

 ek tarah se puraa cinema sansar

 abhinayta ajay devgan apni diwaali par hone ja rahi film 'shivaay' ke ek sho kii puri kamai uri hamale ke peediton ko denge
 Ajay Devgan has asked all the distributors of his film 'shivaay' to give complete information about the collection of all the shows on the first day so that he can give the entire collection of one show to the families of the soldiers killed in the Uri attack
 tippaniyan Talking to NDTV, Ajay Devgan said, 'we have asked all the distributors to give a collection of all the shows on the first day
 'shivaay' kii release ke din kaa jo bhi sabase bada sho hoga yani jis sho se sabase zyada paise aaenge wo sho uri ke peediton ke liye hoga
 That means Ajay Devgan has done a show of the film 'shivaay', which is going to be released this Diwali, after the victims of Uri
 isse pehle cinema onors and aggibitars of india ne apane sadasyon or bollywood nirmaataaon ko ek patr likhakar is diwaali release hone ja rahi film se pehle din pehle sho kii kamai uri hamale main shahid huen phogiyon ke pariwaron ko dene kaa aagrah kiya tha or kaha tha ki hamaari suraksha kar rahe javaanon ke pariwaron kii madad karne ke liye saamne aaiye

 karnataka kaa chunavi ran congress or bijepi ke liye naa sirf 2019 loksabhaa chunaav se pehle semifinal he balki donon partiyon ke liye apni kai ranneetiyon ko aajamaane kii prayogshaala bhi ban gaya he
 The Congress is going to try three major strategies in the field of Karnataka, which are stamped by party president Rahul Gandhi
 1
 Yatra Ek, Lakshya After the success of 'navsarjan Yatra' in many Gujarat, the party's focus in Karnataka has also been on the 'jan Ashirwad Yatra' of Gandhi
 chunaav prachaar ke liye is yatra main rahul bas par rajya se party ke sabhi ahm netaaon ko saath lekar logon se sampark ke liye nikalate hai
 With this, where there is no scope for the leaders to come to the surface of mutual differences, there is a message of the unity of the party among the people
 yatra kaa ye funda rahul ke liye sabase pehle uttar pradesh chunaav ke dauraan chote paimaane par shuru kiya gaya tha
 Then, with full preparation and strategy in Gujarat, the 'navsarjan Yatra' was thrown into full force
 gujarat main nattejey achche saamne aae to karnataka ke mukhyamantri siddharmaiya ne karnataka ke liye bhi prachaar kii aisi hi ranneeti kaa aagrah kiya
